The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
(Published by Authority)
PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government Notifications
1a - PG 6739 - 704 (05/2024) 
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
ARCHITECTS REGISTRATION BOARD
Reference is made to the notes appearing on pages 1a, 2a, 3a, 4a and 5a of the Gazette (extraordinary) No.1015/19 of Friday, 
the 20th February, 1998 of the democratic socialist Republic of sri Lanka with regard to the Registration of persons who are 
eligible to practice architecture in sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered architects”, “architects” and “architectural 
Licentiates”. The interpretations of the sri Lanka Institute of architects (amendment) act, No. 14 of 1996 in the above 
Gazette Notification will apply in all respects to the list published below.
The architects Registration Board as per the functions and powers vested upon it by the section 8B of the act has directed 
me to publish the Register of Chartered architects, architects and architectural Licentiates in compliance with section 8C 
(1) and (2).  This registration is valid until 31st January 2025.
If there are new registrations over the year, such will be included in the Register and can be seen on the updated Register 
published in the ARB official website: www.arb.lk 
N.W.W. Wijekoon,
Registrar,
architects Registration Board,
sri Lanka Institute of architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya mawatha,
Colombo 07.
27 may 2024.
